oṃ namo ratnatrayāya

pathaāyuṣmān ānandaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaram ādāya śrāvastīṃ mahānagarīṃ piṇḍāya prāvikṣat
athaāyuṣmān ānandaḥ śrāvastīṃ piṇḍāya caritvā kṛtabhaktakṛtyo yenānyatamam udapānaṃ tenaupasaṃkrāntaḥ

pmā te putri jīvitaṃ parityajasi ānayāmi śramaṇam ānandam

 icchayā devo varṣati vidyotati gajeti vismayaṃ mahārājasya samabhivardhāyituṃ devebhyo manuṣyebhyo gandharvebhyoḥ śikhigrahā devā viśikhigra

saṃpraharṣayati sma
yeyaṃ kathā dīrgharātraṃ saṃsārasamāpannānāṃ pratikūlā śravaṇīyā
tad yathā
dānakathā śīlakathā svargakathā kāmeṣv

p atha prakṛtir bhikṣuṇī bhagavatā dharmyaya kathayā saṃdarśitā samādāpitā
samuttejitā saṃpraharṣitā hṛṣṭacittā kalyāṇacittā muditacittā vinīvaraṇacittā ṛjucittā
akhilacittā bhavyā dharmadeśitam ājñātum 
p yadā ca bhagavān jñātaḥ prakṛtiṃ bhikṣuṇīṃ hṛṣṭacittāṃ kalyāṇacittāṃ muditacittāṃ
vinivaraṇacittāṃ bhavyāṃ pratibalāṃ sāmutkarpikīṃ dharmadeśanām ājñātuṃ tadā yeyaṃ
bhagavatāṃ buddhānāṃ caturāryasatyaprativedhikī sāmutkarṣikī dharmadeśanā

tad yathā duḥkhaṃ sumudayaṃ nirodhaṃ mārgam

amudācarasiiti

apy aikatyā bhagavatā sārdhaṃ saṃmukhaṃ saṃrañjanīṃ saṃmodinīṃ vividhāṃ kathāṃ vyatisāryaekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ
apy aikasyā bhagavataḥ purataḥ
svakasvakāni mātāpaitṛkāṇi nāmagotrāṇi anuśrāvyaekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ

apy aikatyās tūṣṇīṃ bhūtā ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ
p atha bhagavān rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalam ārabhya teṣāṃ ca saṃbahulānāṃ

pbhikṣavo bhagavantam āhuḥ 
etasya bhagavan kāla etasya sugata samayo yad bhagavān prakṛter bhikṣuṇyāḥ pūrvanivāsam ārabhya dharmakathāṃ kathāyet

vatsānusārī yogaḥ
yuganaddho yogaḥ
tatra nakṣatraṃ yadi purastād gacchati candraś ca pṛṣṭhataḥ
ayam ucyate ṛṣabhānusārī yoga iti
yad uta candraḥ purastād gacchati nakṣatraṃ ca pṛṣṭhataḥ
tadā bhavati vatsānusārī yogaḥ
yadi punaś candro nakṣatraṃ caubhau
samau yugapad gacchataḥ
tadāyam ucyate yuganaddho yoga iti
grahaḥ 
patha khalu bhoḥ puṣkarasārin grahān pravakṣyāmi tac chrūyatāṃ
tad yathā śukro bṛhaspatiḥ śanaiścaro budho aṅgārakaḥ sūryas tārādhipatiś ceti
rātridivasayor hrāsavṛddhī 
pevaṃ viparivartamāne loke nakṣatreṣu pravibhakteṣu kathaṃ rātridivasānāṃ hrāso vṛddhiś ca bhavati tad ucyate
phemantānāṃ dvitīye māsi rohiṇyām aṣṭamyāṃ dvādaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati
aṣṭādaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ
grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse rohiṇyām aṣṭamyām aṣṭādaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati
dvādaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ
varṣāṇāṃ paścime māse rohiṇyām aṣṭamyāṃ caturdaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati
ṣoḍaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ
pkiṃ bhos triśaṅko rātridivasānāṃ prasthānaṃ
divasānudivasaṃ
kiṃ pakṣasya prasthānaṃ
kiṃ saṃvatsarasya prasthānaṃ
pauṣaḥ
kim ṛtūnāṃ prasthānaṃ prāvṛṭ
muhūrtanāmāni 
pkiṃ bhos triśaṅko kṣaṇasya parimāṇaṃ 
kiṃ lavasya
kiṃ muhūrtasya
ptad yathā bhoḥ puṣkarasārin striyā nātidīrghahrasvaḥ kartinyāḥ sūtrodyāmaḥ
evaṃ dīrghas tatkṣaṇaḥ
viṃśatyadhikaṃ tatkṣaṇaśatam ekaḥ kṣaṇaḥ
ṣaṣṭikṣaṇā eko lavaḥ
triṃśallavā eko muhūrtaḥ
etena kramasambandhena triṃśanmuhūrtam ekaṃ rātridivasam anumīyate
teṣāṃ muhūrtānām imāni nāmāni bhavanti
pāditya udayati ṣaṇṇavatipauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ caturojā nāma muhūrto bhavati
ṣaṣṭipauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ śveto nāma muhūrto bhavati
dvādaśapauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ samṛddho nāma muhūrto bhavati
ṣaṭpauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ śarapatho nāma muhūrto bhavati
ppañcapauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyām atisamṛddho nāma muhūrto bhavat
catuḥpauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyām udgato nāma muhūrto bhavati
tripauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ sumukho nāma muhūrto bhavati
sthite madhyāhne vajrako nāma muhūrto bhavati
parivṛtte madhyāhne tripuruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ rohito nāma muhūrto bhavati
pcatuḥpauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ balo nāma muhūrto bhavati
pañcapauruṣāyāṃ chayayaṃ vijayo nāma muhūrtaḥ
ṣaṭpauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ sarvaraso nāma muhūrtaḥ
dvādaśaparuṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ vasur nāma muhūrtaḥ
ṣaṣṭipauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ sundaro nāma muhūrtaḥ
avataramāṇa āditye ṣaṇṇavatipauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ parabhayo nāma muhūrto bhavati
pity etāni divasasya muhūrtāni
patha khalu bhoḥ puṣkarasārin rātryā muhūrtāni vyākhyāsyāmi
astaṃgata āditye raudro nāma muhūrtaḥ
tatas tārāvacaro nāma muhūrtaḥ
saṃyamo nāma muhūrtaḥ 
sāṃpraiyako nāma muhūrtaḥ
ananto nāma muhūrtaḥ
gardabhā nāma muhūrtaḥ
rākṣaso nāma muhūrtaḥ
sthite ardharātre avayavo nāma muhūrtaḥ
atikrānte ardharātre brahmā nāma muhūrtaḥ ditir nāma
muhūrtaḥ ātapāgnir nāma muhūrta
abhijin nāma muhūrtaḥ
ity etāni rātrer muhūrtanāmāni
iti bhoḥ puṣkarasārin imāni triśan muhūrtāni yair ahorātraṃ prajñāyate
ptatkṣaṇaḥ kṣaṇo lavo muhūrtaḥ 
tatra triṃśatitamo bhāgo muhūrtasya lavaḥ
ṣaṣṭitamo bhāgo lavasya kṣaṇaḥ
viṃśatyuttarabhāgaśataṃ kṣaṇasya tatkṣaṇaḥ
tad yathā striyā nātidīrghahrasvaḥ kartinyāḥ sūtrodyāmaḥ
evaṃ dīrghas tatkṣaṇaḥḥ
viṃśatyuttarakṣaṇaśataṃ tatkṣaṇasyaikaḥ kṣaṇaḥ
ṣaṣṭikṣaṇā eko lavaḥ
triṃśallavā eko muhūrtaḥ
etena kramayogena
triṃśanmuhūrtam ekam ahorātraṃ
triṃśad ahorātrāṇy eko māsaḥ
dvādaśamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ
caturojāḥ śvetaḥ samṛddhaḥ śarapatho atisamṛddha udgataḥ 
sumukho vajrako rohito balo vijayaḥ sarvaraso vasuḥ sundaraḥ parabhayaḥ
raudras tārāvacaraḥ saṃyamaḥ sāṃpraiyako annanto gardabho rākṣaso avayavo brahmā ditir arko vidhamano āgneya ātapāgnir abhijit
pitiimāni muhūrtānāṃ nāmāni
kālautpattiḥ 
pabkālotpattim api te brāhmaṇa vakṣyāmi śṛṇu
pcdkālasya kiṃ pramāṇam iti tad ucyate
pdvāvakṣinimeṣāv eko lavaḥ
asṭau lavā ekā kāṣṭhā
ṣoḍaśakāṣṭhā ekā kalā
kalānāṃ triṃśadeko nāḍikā
tatra dve nāḍika eko muhūrtaḥ
pnāḍikāyāḥ punaḥ kiṃ pramāṇaṃ tad ucyate
pdroṇaṃ salilasyaikaṃ
taddharaṇato dve palaśate bhavataḥ
nālikāchidrasya kiṃ pramāṇaṃ
suvarṇamātraṃ
upari caturaṅgulā suvarṇaśalākā kartavyā
 vṛttaparimaṇḍalā samāntāc caturasrā āyatā
yadā caevaṃ śīryeta tat toyaṃ ghaṭasya tadaikā nāḍikā
etena nālikāpramāṇena vibhakte dve nāḍika eko muhūrtaḥ
etena bho brāhmaṇa triṃśan muhūrtāḥ yai
rātridivasā anumīyanta iti
ptataḥ ṣoḍaśa nimeṣā ekā kāṣṭhā
ṣoḍaśa kāṣṭhā ekā kalā
ṣaṣṭikalā eko muhūrtaḥ
triṃśanmuhūrtā ekam ahorātram
triṃśad ahorātrāṇy eko māsaḥ
dvādaśamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ
petena punarakṣinimeṣeṇa ṣoḍaśakoṭayo aṣṭapañcāśac ca śatasahasrāṇi aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi sa evaṃ māpitaḥ
tac ca brāhmaṇa kālotpattir vyākhyātā
krośayojanautpattiḥ 
psṛṇu brāhmaṇa krośayojanānām utpattiṃ
sapta paramāṇava eko aṇur bhavati
saptāṇavaḥ sarvasūkṣmaṃ dṛsyate
tad ekaṃ vātāyanarajaḥ
vātāyanarajāṃsi sapta
śaśakarajaḥ
sapta śaśakarajāṃsy eḍakarajaḥ
sapta eḍakarajāṃśyekaṃ gorajaḥ
saptagorajāṃsy ekā yūkā
saptayūkā ekā likṣā
saptalikṣā eko yavaḥ
sapta yavā ekāṅguliḥ
dvādaśāṅgulayo vitastiḥ
dve vitastī eko hastaḥ
catvāro hastā ekaṃ dhanuḥ
dhanuḥsahasram ekaḥ krośaḥ
catvāraḥ krośā eko māgadhayojanaḥ
yojanasya pramāṇaṃ piṇḍitāṃ
pparamāṇūnāṃ koṭiśatasahasrāṇi caturviṃśatiś caikonatriṃśatkoṭisahasrāṇi dvādaśa ca śatasahasrāṇi
evaṃ māpitaṃ yojanam iti
pśṛṇu brāhmaṇa suvarṇasya parimāṇotpattiṃ
tatkathayatu bhavān
pdvādaśa yavā māṣakaḥ
ṣoḍaśa māsakā ekaḥ karṣaḥ
suvarṇasya parimāṇaṃ piṇḍitam iti
dve koṭī pañcaviṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi pañcaśatāny aṣṭau ca paramāṇavaḥ
evaṃ māpitā brāhmaṇa suvarṇasya parimāṇautpattiḥ
pśṛṇu brāhmaṇa palapramāṇaṃ
catuḥṣaṣṭimāṣakāḥ palaṃ māgadhakaṃ
māgadhakayā tulayā palasya parimāṇaṃ piṇḍitaṃ
paramāṇūnām aṣṭakoṭayaḥ saptacatvāriṃśac ca śatasahasrāṇi sapta ca sahasrāṇi dve śate aśītiś ca paramāṇavaḥ
evaṃ māpitaṃ brāhmaṇa palasya parimāṇam iti
pśṛṇu brāhmaṇa rasaparimāṇasyautpattiṃ
caturviṃśatipalāni māgadhakaḥ
prasthaḥ
tat rasaparimāṇaṃ
māgadhakayā tulayā prasthāsya parimāṇaṃ piṇḍitaṃ
dve koṭiśate tisraś ca koṭaya ekonatiṃśac ca śatasahasrāṇi catuḥsaptati 
sahasrāṇi sapta ca śatāni viṃśatiś ca paramāṇavaḥ
evaṃ māpitā brāhmaṇa rasamānasyautpattir iti
pśṛṇu brāhmaṇa dhānyaparimāṇasyautpattiṃ
ekonatriṃśatipalāny ekakarṣeṇonāni māgadhaḥ prasthaḥ
māpitaṃ dhānyaparimāṇaṃ
māgadhakayā tulayā prasthasya parimāṇaṃ piṇḍitaṃ
koṭiśatam aṣṭapañcāśac ca koṭayo dvir aśītiś ca śata sahasrāṇi ekaṣaṣṭiś ca sahasrāṇi pañcaśatāni triṃśac ca paramāṇavaḥ
evaṃ māpitaṃ brāhmaṇa dhānyasya parimāṇam iti
nakṣatravyākaraṇaṃ
ppaṭha bhos triśaṅko nakṣatravyākaranaṃ nāmaadhyāyaṃ
atha khalu bho brāhmaṇa nakṣatravyākaranaṃ nāmaadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmi
tac chrūyatāṃ
kathayatu bhavān
pkṛttikāsu jāto mānavo yaśasvī bhavati
rohiṇyāṃ jātaḥ subhago bhavati bhogavāṃś ca
mṛgaśirasi jāto yuddhārthī bhavati
ārdrāyāṃ jāta utso annapānānāṃ bhavati
punarvasau jātaḥ kṛṣimān bhavati gorakṣaś ca
puṣye jātaḥ śīlavān bhavati
aśleṣāyāṃ jātaḥ kāmuko bhavati
maghāyāṃ jāto matimān bhavati
mahāātmā ca
pūrvaphalgunyāṃ jāto alpaayuṣko
bhavati uttaraphalgunyāṃ jāta upavāsaśīlo bhavati
svargaparāyaṇaś ca
haste jātaś cauro bhavati
citrāyāṃ jāto nṛtyagītakuśalo bhavati
ābharaṇavidhijñaś ca
svātyāṃ jāto gaṇako bhavati
gaṇakamahāmātro vā
viśākhāyāṃ jāto rājabhaṭo bhavati
anurādhāyāṃ jāto vāṇijako bhavati sārthikaḥ
jyeṣṭhāyāṃ jāto alpaayuṣko bhavati
alpabhogaś ca mūle jātaḥ
putravān bhavati yaśasvī ca
pūrvāṣāḍhāyāṃ jāto yogācāro bhavati
uttarāṣāḍhāyāṃ jāto bhakteśvaraḥ kulīnaś ca bhavati
abhijiti jātaḥ kīrtimān puruṣo bhavati
śravaṇe jāto 
rājapūjito bhavati
dhaniṣṭhāyāṃ jāto dhanāḍhyo bhavati
śatabhiṣāyāṃ jāto mūliko bhavati
pūrvabhādrapadāyāṃ jātaś caurasenāpatir bhavati
uttarabhādrapadāyāṃ jāto gandhiko bhavati
gandharvaś ca
revatyāṃ jāto nāviko bhavati
aśvinyāṃ jāto aśvavāṇijako bhavati
bharaṇyāṃ jāto vadhyaghātako bhavati
ayaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatravyākaraṇo nāma
nakṣatranirdeśaḥ
ppaṭha bhos triśaṅko nakṣatranirdeśaṃ nāmaadhyāyaṃ
atha bhoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatranirdeśaṃ nāmaadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmi tac chrūyatāṃ 
kathayatu bhavān
pabkṛttikāsu niviṣṭaṃ vai nagaraṃ jvalati śriyā
pcdprabhūratnojvalaṃ caeva tan nagaraṃ vinirdiśet
pabrohiṇyāṃ tu niviṣṭaṃ vai nagaraṃ tad vinirdiśet
pcddhārmiko atra jano bhūyāt prabhūtadhanasañcayaḥ
pefvidyāprakṛtisampannaḥ svadārābhir ato api ca
pabmṛgaśīrṣe niviṣṭaṃ tu strībhir gobhir dhanais tathā
pcdmālyabhogaiś ca saṅkīrṇam adbhutaiś ca puraskṛtaṃ
pabārdrāyāṃ matsyamāṃsāni bhakṣyabhojyadhanāni ca
pcdbhavanti krūrapuruṣā mūrkhaprakṛtayaḥ pure
pabpunarvasau niviṣṭe tu nagaraṃ dīpyate śriyā
pcdprabhūtadhanadhānyaṃ ca bhūtvā vāapi vinaśyati
pabsrīmatpuṣye niviṣṭe tu prajā duṣṭā prasīdati
pcdyuktāḥ śriyā ca dharmiṣṭhās tathiva cirajīvinaḥ
pabtejasvinaś ca dīrghāyurdhanadhānyarasānvitāḥ
pcdvanaspatis tathā kṣipraṃ puṣyet tatra punaḥ punaḥ
pabaśleṣāyāṃ niviṣṭe tu durbhagāḥ kalahapriyāḥ
pcdduḥśīlā duḥkhabhājaś ca nivasanti narādhamāḥ
pabmaghāyāṃ ca niviṣṭe tu vidyāvanto mahādhanāḥ
pcdsvadārāabhiratā martyā jāyante suparākramāḥ
pabphalgunyāṃ tu striyo mālyaṃ bhojanācchādanaṃ śubhaṃ
pcdgandhopetāni dhanyāni niviṣṭe nagare bhavet
pabuttarāyāṃ tu phālgunyāṃ dhānyāni ca dhanāni ca
pcdmūrkhā janā jitāḥ strībhir niviṣṭe nagare bhavet
pabhaste ca viniviṣṭe tu vidyāvanto mahādhanāḥ
pcdparasparaṃ ca rucitaṃ śayanaṃ nagare bhavet
pabcitrāyāṃ ca niviṣṭe tu strījitāḥ sarvamānavāḥ
pcdśrīmatkāntaṃ ca nagaraṃ jvalantaṃ tad vinirdiśet
pabsvātyāṃ pure niviṣṭe tu prabhūtadhanasañcayāḥ
pcdlubdhāḥ krūrāś ca mūrkhāś ca prabhūtā nagare bhavet
pabviśākhāyāṃ niviṣṭaṃ tu nagaraṃ jvalati śriyā
pcdyāyajūkajanākīrṇaṃ śastrāntaṃ ca vinirdiśed
pabanurādhāniviṣṭe tu dharmaśīlā jitendriyāḥ
pcdsvadāraniratāḥ puṇyā japahomaparāyaṇāḥ
pabjyeṣṭhāyāṃ sanniviṣṭaṃ tu bahuratnadhanānvitaiḥ
pcdsattvair vedavidaiḥ pūrṇaṃ śaśvatsamabhivardhate
pabmūlena saniviṣṭaṃ tu puraṃ dhānyadhanānvitaṃ
pcdduḥśīlajanasaṅkīrṇaṃ pāṃsunā ca vinaśyati
pabpūrvāṣāḍhāniviṣṭaṃ tu puraṃ syād dhanadhānyabhāk
pcdlubdhāḥ krūrāś ca mūrkhāś ca nivasanti narādhamāḥ
pabniviṣṭe tūttarāyāṃ ca dhanadhānyasamuccayaḥ
pcdvidyāprakṛtisampanno janaś ca kalahapriyaḥ
pababhijiti niviṣṭe tu nagare tatra moditāḥ
pcdnarāḥ sarve sadā hṛṣṭāḥ parasparānurāgiṇaḥ
pabśravaṇāyāṃ niviṣṭaṃ tu puraṃ dhānyadhanānvitaṃ
pcdarogijanabhūyiṣṭhasahitaṃ tad vinirdiśet
pabdhaniṣṭhāyāṃ niviṣṭaṃ tu strījitaṃ puram ādiśet
pcdprabhūtavastramālyaṃ ca kāmabhogavivirjitam
pabpure śatabhiṣāyukta mūrkhaśāṭhyapriyā jahāḥ
pcdstrīṣu pāneṣu saṃsaktāḥ salilena vinaśyati
pabpure proṣṭhapadādhyakṣe narās tatra sukhapriyāḥ
pcdparopatāpino mūrkhā mānakāmavivarjitāḥ
pabuttarāyāṃ niviṣṭe tu śaśvadvṛddhir anuttarā
pcdpūrṇaṃ ca dhanadhānyābhyāṃ ratnāḍhyaṃ ca vinirdiśet
pabpure niviṣṭe raivatyāṃ sundarī janatā bhavet
pcdkharoṣṭraṃ caeva gāvaś ca prabhūtadhanadhānyatā
pabaśvinyāṃ viniviṣṭaṃ tu nagaraṃ śivam ādiśet
pcdarogijanasampūrṇaṃ darśanīyajanākulam
pabbharaṇyāṃ sanniviṣṭe tu durbhagāḥ kalahapriyāḥ
pcdduḥśīlā duḥkhabhājaś ca vasanti puruṣādhamāḥ
pabpurāṇi rāṣṭraṇi tathā gṛhāṇi nakṣatrayogaṃ prasamīkṣya vidvān
pcdiṣṭe praśaste ca niveśayet tu pūrve ca janme adhigataṃ mayedaṃ
payaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatranirdeśo nāmaadhyāyaḥ
nakṣatrāṇāṃ sthānanirdeśaḥ
patha khalu bhoḥ puṣkarasārinn aṣṭāviṃśatīnāṃh
nakṣatrāṇāṃ sthānanirdeśaṃ nāmaadhyāyaṃ pravakṣyāmi
etac chrūyatāṃ
pkathayatu bhagavān
pkṛttikā bhoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatraṃ kaliṅgamagadhānāṃ 
rohiṇī sarvaprajāyāḥ
mṛgaśirā videhānāṃ rājopasevakānāṃ ca
evam ārdrā kṣatriyāṇāṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ ca
punarvasuḥ sauparṇānāṃ
puṣyanakṣatraṃ sarveṣām avadātavadātavasanānāṃ
rājapadasevakānāṃ ca
aśleṣā nāgānāṃ haimavatānāṃ ca
maghānakṣatraṃ gauḍikānāṃ
pūrvaphalgunī caurāṇāṃ
uttaraphalgunī
avantīnāṃ hastā saurāṣṭrikāṇāṃ
citrā pakṣiṇāṃ dvipadānāṃ
svātī sarveṣāṃ pravrajyāsamāpannānāṃ
viśākhā audakānāṃ
anurādhā vāṇijakānāṃ śākaṭikānāṃ ca
jyeṣṭhā dauvālikānāṃ
 mūlā pathikānāṃ
pūrvāṣāḍhā vāhlīkānāṃ ca
uttarāṣāḍhā kāmbojānāṃ
abhijit sarveṣāṃ dakṣiṇāpathikānāṃ tāmraparṇikānāṃ ca
śravaṇā ghādakānāṃ caurāṇāṃ ca
dhaniṣṭhā kurupāñcālānāṃ
śatabhiṣā maulikānām ārthavaṇikānāṃ ca
pūrvabhādrapadā gandhikānāṃ yavanakāmbojānāṃ ca
uttarabhādrapadā gandharvāṇāṃ
revatī nāvikānāṃ ca
aśvinī aśvavāṇijānāṃ ca
bharaṇī bhadrapadakarmaṇāṃ bhadrakāyākānāṃ ca
payaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatrāṇāṃ sthānanirdeśavyākaraṇo nāmaadhyāyaḥ
ṛtuvarṣaḥ
ppaṭha bhos triśaṅko ṛtuvarṣaṃ nāmaadhyāyaṃ
tad ahaṃ vakṣye śrūyatāṃ
kathayatu bhagavān
pkṛttikāsu grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
varṣo daśarātrikaḥ
śravaṇāyuktaproṣṭhapadāyām agnodako varṣārātro bhavati
paścād varṣaṃ saṃjanayati
hemante grīṣme grīṇi caatra 
bhayapragrahāṇi bhavanti
agnibhayaṃ śastrabhayaṃ caudakabhayaṃ ca bhavati
uktaṃ kṛttikāsu
prohiṇyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ekaviṃśatyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
tatra nimnāni kṛṣikartavyāni
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni
eṣa ca varṣārātraḥ sāroparodhaḥ sasyaṃ ca saṃpādayati
dvau caatra rogau prabalau bhavataḥ
kukṣirogaś cakṣūrogaś ca
caurabahulāś caatra diśo bhavanti
uktaṃ ca rohiṇyāṃ
pmṛgaśirasi grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
sāroparodho varṣārātraḥ
paścād varṣaṃ saṃjanayati
nikṣiptaśastrāś caatra 
rājāno bhavanti
kṣemiṇaḥ sunītikāś ca diśo bhavanti
muditāś caatra janapadā bhavanti
uktaṃ mṛgaśirasi
pārdrāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati aṣṭādaśāḍhakāni pravarṣati
tatra nimnāni kṛṣikartavyāni
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni
nidhayaś ca rakṣayitavyāḥ
caurabahulāś caatra diśo bhavanti
nikṣiptaśastrāś ca rājāno bhavanti
trayaś caatra rogāḥ prabalā bhavanti
jvaraḥ śvāso galagrahaś ca
bālānāṃ dārakadārikāṇāṃ ca maraṇaṃ
bhavati ity uktam ārdrāyāṃ
ppunarvasau grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati
navatyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
mahāmeghān utpādayati
āṣāḍhāyāṃ praviṣṭāyāṃ mṛdūni pravarṣati
anantaraṃ ca nirantareṇa pravarṣati
nikṣiptaśastrāś ca rājāno bhavanti
uktaṃ punarvasau
ppuṣye grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati dvātriṃśadāḍhakāni pravarṣati
atra nimnāni kṛṣikartavyāni
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni
vyaktaṃ pradhānavarṣāṇi bhavanti
sasyaṃ ca niṣpādayati
brāhmaṇakṣatriyāṇāṃ ca virodho bhavati
daṃṣṭriṇaś caatra prabalā bhavanti
tatra trayo rogāś ca bhavanti
gaṇḍāḥ piṭakāḥ pāmāni ca  ity uktaṃ
puṣye
paśleṣāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ekaviṃśatyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
tatra nimnāni kṛṣikartavyāni
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni
viṣamāś ca vāyavo vānti
saṃvignāś caatra jñānino rājānaś ca bhavanti
eṣo varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni sampādayati
jāyāpatikānāṃ rājāmātyānāṃ ca virodho bhavati
uktam aśleṣāyāṃ
pmaghāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni 
pravarṣati
eṣo varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni sampādayati
mṛgapakṣipaśumanuṣyāṇāṃ caatra garbhā vinaśyanti
janamaraṇaṃ caatra bhaviṣyatiiti
uktaṃ maghāyāṃ
ppūrvaphalgunyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
eṣo varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni sampādayati
tac ca sasyaṃ janayitvā paracakrapīḍitā manuṣyā na sukhenopabhuñjate
paśūnāṃ maṇuṣyāṇāṃ caatra garbhāḥ sukhino bhavanti
uktaṃ pūrvaphalgunyāṃ
puttaraphalgunyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati aśītyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
eṣo varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni ca sampādayati
nikṣiptaśastrāś caatra rājāno bhavanti
brahmakṣatriyayoś ca virodho bhavati
kṣipraṃ ca anītikāḥ prajā vinaśyanti
cauktam uttaraphalgunyāṃ
phaste grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ekonapañcāśadāḍhakāni 
pravarṣati
devaś ca tad yathā parikṣipati
patitāni ca sasyāni janasyārasāgrāṇi anudagrāṇi alpasārāṇy alpodakāni
durbhikṣaś caatra bhaviṣyati
uktaṃ haste
pcitrāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
sāroparodhas tataḥ paścād varṣaṃ saṃjanayati
nikṣiptaśastrāś ca rājāno bhavanti
muditāś caatra janapadā bhavanti
uktaṃ citrāyāṃ
psvātyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ekaviṃśatyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
nikṣiptaśastrāś ca rājāno bhavanti
caurāś caatra balavattarā bhavanti
uktaṃ svātyāṃ
pviśākhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati aśītyāḍhakāni 
pravarṣati
eṣā varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni sampādayati
rājānaś caatra chidrayuktā bhavanti
agnidāhāś caatra prabalā bhavanti
daṃṣṭriṇaś caatra balavanto api kṣayaṃ gacchanti
uktaṃ viśākhāyāṃ
panurādhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
eṣo varṣaḥ sasyaṃ sampādayati
mitrāṇi caatra dṛḍhāni bhavanti
uktam anurādhāyāṃ
pjyeṣṭhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ṣoḍaśāḍhakāni pravarṣati
tatra kṛṣikarmān tāni pratisaṃhartavyāni
yugavaratrāṇi varjayitavyāni
svadhānyāni upasaṃhartavyāni
agnayaḥ pratisaṃhartavyāḥ
lāṅgalāni pratisaṃhartavyāni
avaśyam anena janapadena vinaṣṭavyaṃ bhavati
paracakrapīḍito bhavati
uktaṃ jyeṣṭhāyāṃ
pmūle grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati catuṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni 
pravarṣati
eṣo varṣaḥ sasyaṃ sampādayati
caurabahulāś caatra diśo bhavanti
trayaś caatra vyādhayo balavanto bhavanti
vātagaṇḍaḥ pārśvaśūlam akṣirogaś ca
puṣpaphalāni caatra samṛddhāni bhavanti
nikṣiptaśastrāś caatra rājāno bhavanti uktaṃ mūle
ppūrvasyām āṣāḍhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
dvau caatra grāhau bhavataḥ 
proṣṭhapade vā aśvayujau vā pakṣe
eṣo varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni sampādayati
dvau caatra rogau prabalau bhavataḥ
kukṣirogo akṣirogaś ca 
uktaṃ pūrvāṣāḍhāyāṃ
puttarasyām āṣāḍhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati pūrṇam āḍhakaśataṃ pravarṣati
tatra sthalāni kṛṣikartavyāni
nimnāni parivarjayitavyāni
mahāsrotāṃsi caatra pravahanti
agrodakā caatra varṣā bhavati
sarvasasyāni niṣpādayati
trayaś caatra rogāḥ prabalā bhavanti
gaṇḍaḥ kacchaḥ kaṇṭharoga iti
uktam uttarāṣāḍhāyām
pabhijiti grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra pravarṣati catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhākāni 
pravarṣati
maṇḍalavarṣaṃ ca devaḥ pravarṣati
paścād varṣaḥ sasyaṃ janayati
audakānāṃ bhūtānām utsargo bhavati
uktam abhijiti
pśravaṇe tu grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati catuṣṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
maṇḍalavarṣaṃ ca devo varṣati
paścād varṣā sasyaṃ sampādayati
audakānāṃ bhūtānām utsargo bhavati
vyādhibahulāś ca narā bhavanti
rājānaś ca tīvradaṇḍā bhavanti
uktaṃ śravaṇe
pdhaniṣṭhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ekapañcāśadāḍhakāni pravarṣati
vibhaktāś caatra varṣā bhavanti
tatra nimnāni kṛṣikartavyāni
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni
durmukho rātrau varṣo bhavati
sasyāni sampādayati
ekaś caatra rogo bhavati
gaṇḍavikāraḥ
śastrasamādānāś ca rājāno bhavanti
uktaṃ dhaniṣṭhāyāṃ
pśatabhiṣāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ṣoḍaśāḍhakāni 
pravarṣati
tatra nimnāni kṛṣikartavyāni
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni
eṣo varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni sampādayati
cakrasamārūḍhā janapadā bhavanti
manuṣyā dārakadārikāś ca skandhe kṛtvā deśaantaraṃ gacchanti
uktaṃ śatabhiṣāyaṃ
ppūrvasyāṃ bhādrapadāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
varṣāmukhe caatra ekonaviṃśati rātriko avagraho bhavati
puṣpasasyaṃ ca nāśayati
etāś ca varṣā bahucaurā bhavanti
dvau caatra mahāvyādhī bhavataḥ
prathamaṃ pittatāpajvaro bhavati
paścād balavān mahāgraho bhavati
martyānāṃ nārīṇāṃ
ca maraṇaṃ bhavati
uktaṃ pūrvabhādrapadāyāṃ
puttarasyāṃ bhādrapadāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati pūrṇam āḍhakaśataṃ pravarṣati
mahāsrotāṃsi pravahanti
grāmanagaranigamāḥ srotasā uhyante
catvāraś caatra vyādhayaḥ prabalā bhavanti
tad yathā kukṣirogo akṣirogaḥ 
kāśo jvaraś ceti
bālānāṃ dārakadārikāṇāṃ maraṇāṃ bhavati
atra sthalāni kṛṣikartavyāni nimnāni
parivarjayitavyāni
etāś ca varṣāḥ puṣpāṇi phalāni ca sampādayanti
uktam uttarabhādrapadāyāṃ
prevatyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati ekaṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati
tatra nimnāni kṛṣikartavyāni
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni
eṣā paribhuñjate
nikṣiptaśastradaṇḍāś ca rājāno bhavanti
anudvignāś ca janapadā bhavanti
udvignāś ca dānapatayo bhavanti
devanakṣatrasamāyuktāś ca janapadā bhavanti
mitrāṇi samāyuktāni bhavanti
uktaṃ revatyāṃ
paśvinyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati aṣṭacatvāriṃśadāḍhakāni pravarṣati
yac ca madhye varṣā bhavati
tatra nimnāni kṛṣikartavyāni
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni
eṣā varṣā sarvasasyāni sampādayati
 bhayasamāyuktāś caatra janapadā bhavanti
caurāś ca prabalā bhavanti
uktam aśvinyāṃ
pbharaṇyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yady atra devaḥ pravarṣati pūrṇam āḍhakaśataṃ pravarṣati
tatra sthalāni kṛṣikartavyāni
nimnāni parivarjayitavyāni
durbhikṣas caatra bhavati
jarāmaraṇaṃ janānāṃ bhavati
rājānaś caatra anyonyaghātakā bhavanti
putrapautrāṇāṃ ca kalaho bhavati
uktaṃ bharaṇyāṃ
payaṃ ghoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatrartuvarṣādhyāyaḥ
 rāhugrahe phalavipākaḥ
pamīṣāṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārinn aśṭāviṃśatīnāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ rāhugrahe phalavipākaṃ vyākhyāsyāmi
pkṛttikāsu bhoḥ puṣkarasārin yadi candragraho bhavati kaliṅgamagadhānām upapīḍā bhavati
yadi rohiṇyāṃ candragraho bhavati prajānām upapīḍā bhavati
yadi mṛgaśirasi candragraho bhavati videhānāṃ janapadānām upapīḍā bhavati
rājopasevakanāṃ ca
evam ārdrāyāṃ punarvasau puṣye ca vaktavyaṃ
aśleṣāyāṃ yadi candragraho bhavati nāgānāṃ haimavatānāṃ
ca pīḍā bhavati
yadi maghāsu candragraho bhavati gauḍikānām upapīḍā bhavati
yadi pūrvaphalgunyāṃ somo gṛhyate caurāṇām upapīḍā  bhavati
yady uttaraphalgunyāṃ somo gṛhyate avantīnām upapīḍā bhavati
yadi hasteṣu somo gṛhyate saurāṣṭrikāṇām upapīḍā bhavati
yadi citrāyāṃ somo gṛhyate pakṣiṇāṃ dvipadānāṃ ca pīḍā bhavati
yadi svātyāṃ somo gṛhyate
sarveṣāṃ pravrajyāsamāpannānām upapīḍā bhavati
yady anurādhāsu somo gṛhyate vaṇijānām upapīḍā bhavati śākaṭikānāṃ ca
yadi jyeṣṭhāyāṃ somo gṛhyate dauvālikānāṃ pīḍā bhavati
yadi mūle somo gṛhyate adhvagānāṃ pīḍā bhavati
yadi pūrvāṣāḍhāyāṃ somo gṛhyate avantīnāṃ pīḍā bhavati
yady uttarāṣāḍhāyāṃ somo gṛhyate kāmbojakānāṃ pīḍā bhavati
bāhlīkānāṃ ca
yady abhijiti somo gṛhyate dakṣiṇāpathikānāṃ pīḍā bhavati
tāmraparṇikānāṃ ca
yadi śravaṇeṣu somo gṛhyate caurāṇāṃ ghātakānāṃ caupapīḍā bhavati
yadi dhaniṣṭhāyāṃ somo gṛhyate kurupāñcālanāṃ pīḍā bhavati
yadi śatabhiṣāyāṃ somo gṛhyate maulikānām ātharvaṇikānāṃ ca pīḍā bhavati
yadi pūrvabhādrapadāyāṃ somo gṛhyate gāndhikānāṃ yavanakāmbojakānāṃ ca pīḍā
bhavati yady uttarabhādrapadāyāṃ somo gṛhyate 
gandharvāṇāṃ pīḍā bhavati
yadi revatyāṃ somo gṛhyate nāvikānāṃ pīḍā bhavati
yady aścviṇijānāṃ pīḍā bhavati
yadi bharaṇyāṃ somo gṛhyate bharukacchānāṃ pīḍā bhavati
pevaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatre candragraho bhavati tasya tasya deśasya pīḍā bhavati
ity ukto rāhugrahaphalavipākādhyāyaḥ
 nakṣatrakarmanirdeśaḥ
ppratinakṣatravaṃśaśāstre yathoktaṃ karma tac chṛṇu
pabucyamānam idaṃ vipra
ṛṣīṇāṃ vacanaṃ yathā
pcdṣaṭtārāṃ kṛttikāṃ vidyād āśrayaṃ tāsu kārayet
pefagnyādhānaṃ pākayajñaḥ samṛddhiprasavaś ca yaḥ
pabsarpirviloḍayet tatra gavāṃ veśma ca kārayet
pcdajaiḍakāś ca kretavyā gavāṃ ca vṛṣam utsṛjet
pabaśmasāramayaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ sarvam atra tu kārayet
pcdhiraṇyakārakarmaantamiṣv astraṃ caupakārayet
pabmetṛko māpayed atra kuṭikāgniniveśanaṃ
pcdpītalohitapuṣpāṇāṃ bījāny atra tu ghāpayet
pabgṛhaṃ ca māpayet atra tathā avāsaṃ prakalpayet
pcdnavaṃ ca chādayed vastraṃ krayaṇaṃ naatra kārayet
pabkrūrakarmāṇi sidhyanti yuddhasaṃrodhabandhanam
pcdparapīḍām athātraiva vidvān naiva prayojayet
pabśastrāṇi kṣurakarmāṇi sarvāṇy atra tu kārayet
pcdtejasāni ca bhāṇḍāni kārayec ca krīṇīta ca
pabāyuṣyaṃ ca śiraḥsnānāṃ strīṇāṃ viṣkambhaṇāni ca
pcdpravarṣaṇaṃ ced devasya naatra vairaṃ praśāmyati
pabkrodhano harṣaṇaḥ śūras tejasvī sāhasapriyaḥ
pcdāyuṣmāṃś ca yaśasvī ca yajñaśīlo atra jāyatekṛttikāsu
pabsarvaṃ kṛṣipadaṃ karma rohiṇyāṃ saṃprayojayet
pcdkṣetravastuvihārāṃś ca navaṃ veśma ca kārayet
pabprayojayec cakrān vārān dāsāṃś caeva gṛhe paśūn
pcdvāpayet sarvabījāni dhruvaṃ vāsāṃsi kārayet
pabṛṇaṃ na dadyāt tatraeva vairam atra tu vardhate
pcdsaṃgrāmaṃ ca surāyogaṃ dvayam eva vivarjayet
pabpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya janma caatra praśasyate
pcdsānukrośaḥ kṣamāyuktaḥ strīkāmo bhakṣalolupaḥ
pefāyuṣmān paśumān dhanyo mahābhogo atra jāyaterohiṇyāṃ
pabsaumyaṃ mṛgaśiro vidyād ṛju tisraś ca tārakāḥ
pcdmṛdūni yāni karmāṇi tāni sarvāṇi kārayet
pefyāni karmāṇi rohiṇyāṃ tāni sarvāṇi kārayet
pabsakṣīrān vāpayed vṛkṣān bījāni kṣīravanti ca
pcdrājaprāsādavalabhīchatrāṇy api ca kārayet
pabsarvakarmakathāḥ kuryāc caryāvāsān na kārayet
pcduṣṭrāṃś ca balīvardāṃś ca damayed api kṛṣṭaye
pabācchādayen navaṃ vāsaś caalaṅkāraṃ ca kārayet
pcddvijātīnāṃ tu karmāṇi sarvāṇy evātra kārayet
pabpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya suvṛṣṭiṃ caatra nirdiśet
pcdsvapnaśīlas tathā trāsī medhāvī sa ca jāyate
mṛgaśirasi
pabārdrāyāṃ mṛgayed arthān bhadraṃ karma ca kārayet
pcdkrūrakarmāṇi sidhyanti tāni vidvān vivarjayet
pabudapānaparīkhāṃś ca taḍāgāny atra kārayet
prathamāṃ vṛṣṭiṃ vikrīṇīyāc ca naatra gāṃ
peftilapīḍāni karmāṇi śauṇḍikānāṃ tathāpaṇaṃ
pabpīḍayed ikṣudaṇḍāni
ikṣubījāni vāpayet
pcdpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya vidyād bahuparisravaṃ
pefkrodhano mṛgayāśīlo māmsakāmo atra jāyateārdrāyāṃ
pabpunarvasau tu yukte atra kuryād vai vratadhāraṇaṃ
pcdgodānaṃ caupanāyanaṃ sarvam atra prasidhyati
pabprajāyamānāṃ pramadāṃ gṛhītvā gṛham ānayet
pcdpunaḥ punar yadīccheta tatra karmāṇi kārayet
pabcikitsanaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchen na parābhavaṃ
pcdpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya janma caatra praśasyate
pabalīlaś caatra jāyeta strīlolaś caapi mānavaḥ
pcdcitraśīlaś ca naikatrārpitacittaḥ sa ucyate
punarvasau
pabdhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ puṣye nityaṃ prayojayet
pcdsarveṣāṃ ca dvijātīnāṃ sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
pabrājāmātyaṃ prayuñjīta śuśrūṣāṃ vinayaṃ caret
pcdrājānam abhipiñced ca
alaṃkuryāt svakāṃ tanu
pabśmaśrukarmāṇi kuryāc ca vapanaṃ nakhalomataḥ
pcdpurohitaṃ ca kurvīta dhvajaagraṃ ca prakārayet
pabpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya mandavarṣaṃ samādiśet
pcdna ca rogo na cauraś ca kṣemaṃ caatra sadā bhavet
pabpuṣyeṇa nityayuktaḥ san sarvakarmāṇi sādhayet
pcdvaireṇātropanāhaiś ca ye janās tān vivarjayet
pefāyuṣmāṃś ca yaśasvī ca mahābhogaḥ prajāyatepuṣye
pabsidhyate dāruṇaṃ karma
aśleṣāyāṃ ca kārayet
pcdkuryād ābharaṇāny atra prākāram upakalpayet
pabdehabandhaṃ nadībandhaṃ sandhikarma ca kārayet
pcdprabhūtadaṃśamaśakaṃ varṣaṃ mandaṃ ca varṣati
pefkrodhanaḥ svapnaśīlaś ca kuhakaś caatra jāyateaśleṣāyāṃ
pabmaghāsu sarvadhānyāni vāpayet saṃhared api
pcdsaṃghātakarma kurvīta sumukhaṃ caatra kārayet
pabkoṣṭhaāgārāṇi kurvīta phalaṃ caatra niveśayat
pcdsarvadā pitṛdevebhyaḥ śrāddhaṃ caivaatra kārayet
pabsasyānāṃ bahulībhāvo yadi devo atra varṣati
pcdsuhṛc ca dvārikaś caeva rasakāmaś ca jāyate
pefāyuṣmān bahuputraś ca strīkāmo bhaktalolupaḥ
pabsaṃgrāmaṃ jīyate tatra yadi pūrvaṃ pravartate
pcddāruṇāni ca karmāṇi tāni vidvān vivarjayetmaghāsu
pabphalgunīṣu ca pūrvāsu saubhāgyārthāni kārayet
pcdviśeṣād āmalakyādi phalānām upakārayet
pabkumārīmaṅgalārthāni snāpanāni ca kārayet
pcdkanyāpravahanārthāya vihāraṃ caeva kārayet
pabveśmāni kārayet tatra vaśyavaiśya
m atra prayojayet
pcdbhāgaṃ ye caupajīvanti teṣāṃ karma prayojayet
pabavyaktakeśo akeśaḥ subhagaś caatra jāyate
pcdpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya suvṛṣṭim abhinirdiśet
pefnaṣṭaṃ viddhaṃ kṛtaṃ caapi na tad astiiti nirdiśet
pūrvaphalgunyāṃ
pabuttarāyāṃ tu phalgunyāṃ sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
pcdmedhāvī darśanīyaś ca yaśasvī caatra jāyate
pabathātra naṣṭaṃ dagdhaṃ vā sarvam astiiti nirdiśet
pcdpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya vidyāt saṃpadanuttamāṃ
uttaraphalgunyāṃ
pabhastena laghukarmāṇi sarvāṇy eva prayojayet
pcdsarveṣāṃ ca dvijātīnāṃ sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
pabhastyārohaṃ mahāmātraṃ puṣkariṇīṃ ca kārayet
pcdcauryaṃ ca sidhyate tatra tac ca vidvān vivarjayet
pabpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya varṣā viśrāvaṇī bhavet
pcdathātra jātaṃ jānīyāc chūraṃ cauraṃ vicakṣaṇaṃ
pefkuśalaṃ sarvavidyāsu
ārogaṃ cirajīvinaṃhaste
pabcitrāyām āhataṃ vastraṃ bhūṣaṇāni ca kārayet
pcdrājānaṃ bhūṣitaṃ paśyet senāvyūhaṃ ca darśayet
pabhiraṇyaṃ rajataṃ dravyaṃ nagarāṇi ca māpayet
pcdalaṅkuryāt tathātmānaṃ gandhamālyavilepanaiḥ
pabgaṇakānāṃ ca vidyāṃ ca vādyaṃ nartanagāyanaṃ
pcdpūrvikāṃ rūpakārāṃś ca rathakārāṃś ca śikṣayet
pefcitrakarāṃś ca lekhakān pustakarma ca kārayet
pabpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya citravarṣaṃ vinirdiśet
pcdmedhāvī darśanīyaś ca citrākṣo bhaktalolupaḥ
pabmṛduśīlaś ca bhīruś ca calacittaḥ kutūhalī
pcdāyuṣmān subhagaś caeva strīlolaś caatra jāyatecitrāyāṃ
pabsvātyāṃ prayojayed yodhān aśvān aśvatarīṃ kharān
pcdkṣipraṃ gamanīyaṃ bhakṣyaṃ laṅghakān adhvamānikān
pabbherīmṛdaṅgapaṇavān murajān caupanāhayet
pcdāvāhaṃś ca vivāhaṃś ca sauhṛdyaṃ caatra kārayet
pabnirvāsanam amitrāṇāṃ svayaṃ na pravased gṛhāt
pcdpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya vātavṛṣṭir abhīkṣṇaśaḥ
pefmedhāvī rogabahulaś calacittaś ca jāyatesvātau
pablāṅgalāni viśākhāsu karṣaṇaṃ ca prayojayet
pcdyavagodhūmakarmaantān śamīdhānyaṃ ca varjayet
pabśālayas tilamāṣāś ca ye ca vṛkṣāḥ suśākhinaḥ
pabropayet tān viśākhāsu gṛhakarma ca kārayet
pcdśiraḥsnānāni kurvīta medhyaṃ prāyaś ca kārayet
pabpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya vidyāt kalpaparisravaṃ
pcdmanasvī darśanīyaś ca medhāvī caatra jāyate
pefkrodhano alpasutaś caeva durbhago bhaktalolupaḥviśākhāsu
pabanurādhāsu kurvīta mitraiḥ sadbhiś ca saṅgatiṃ
pcdsarvāṇi mṛdukarmāṇi mādhuryaṃ caatra kārayet
pabkṣauraṃ ca kārayet atra śastrakarmāṇi kārayet
pcdsaṃyuktāntaprayogāṃś ca sandhiṃ kuryāc ca nityaśaḥ
pefnaṣṭaṃ paryupataptaṃ vā svalpāyasenayāsaṃvinirdiśet
pabsuhṛnmitrakṛtaś caatra dharmaśīlaś ca jāyate
pcdpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya suvṛṣṭim abhinirdiśet
anurādhāyāṃ
pabjyeṣṭhāyāṃ pūrvakārī syād rājānaṃ caabhiṣiñcayet
pcdnagaraṃ nigamaṃ grāmaṃ māpayed ārabheta ca
pefkṣatriyāṇāṃ ca rājñāṃ ca sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
pabbhrātṛṇāṃ bhavati jyeṣṭho jyeṣṭāyāṃ yo abhijāyate
pcdāyuṣmāṃś ca yaśasvī ca vidvatsu ca kutūhalī
pabprāsādam ārohec caatra gajam aśvaṃ rathaṃ tathā
pcdgrāmanigamarāṣṭreṣu sthāpayec chreṣṭhināṃ balaṃ
pabnaṣṭaṃ paryupataptaṃ vā kleśenaiveti nirdiśet
pcddāruṇāny atra sidhyanti tāni vidvān vivarjayet
pefpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya suvṛṣṭim abhinirdiśet
jyeṣṭhāyāṃ
pabmūle tu mūlajātāni mūlakandālukāny api
pcdsūlādyāni ca sarvāṇi bījāny atra prayojayet
pabṛṇaṃ vai yat purāṇaṃ syād artho caasyāgrataḥ sthitaḥ
pcdmūle siddhartham ārabhyaṃ tathā sarvaṃ varāṅgakaṃ
pabcikitsitāni yānīha strīṇāṃ dārakakanyayoḥ
pcdnadīṣu snapanaṃ caeva mūle sarvān prayojayet
pabdāruṇāny atra sidhyanti maṅgalāni ca kārayet
pcdkiṇvayogān surāyogān na kuryāc chatrubhiḥ saha
pabdhanavān bahuputraś ca mūlavān atra jāyate
pcdathātra naṣṭaṃ dagdhaṃ vā naitad astiiti nirdiśet
pefpravarṣaṇaṃ ca devasya suvṛṣṭim abhinirdiśetmūle
pabāṣāḍhāyāṃ ca pūrvasyāṃ saritaś ca sarāṃsi ca
pcdvāpīkūpaprapāś caeva taḍāgāni ca kārayet
pabutpādyāni ca puṣpāṇi tathā mūlaphalāni ca
pcdārāmāṃś ca prakurvīta bhaikṣakāṃś ca prayojayet
pefyāni caugrāṇi karmāṇi sidhyanty atra tu tāni ca
pabnaṣṭaṃ paryupataptaṃ vā naitad astiiti nirdiśet
pcdāyuṣmān puṇyaśīlaś ca darśanīyo atra jāyate
pūrvāṣāḍhe
pabuttarasyām āṣāḍhāyāṃ vairāṇi na samācaret
pcdvāyayet sarvavāsāṃsi navaṃ nācchādayed iti
pabna saṃhared bhedayed vā vāstukarma na sidhyati
pcdśālākarma gavaādīnāṃ grāme grāmaṇinas tathā
pcśreṇavindhaṃ ca rājā nu samayaṃ caatra kārayet
pabpragalbhaś ca sabhāśīlaḥ kṛtī caatra prajāyate
pcdsuhṛdām abhiyogī ca mantrabhāṣye vicakṣaṇaḥ
pabnaṣṭaṃ vāapy upataptaṃ vā
astīty evaṃ vinirdiśet

uttarāṣāḍhāyāṃ

pabkarṇayor vedhanaṃ kuryād rājānaṃ caabhiṣiñcayet

pcdmedhāvī arogī balavān yajñaśīlo atra jāyate

pabdhaniṣṭhā laghu nakṣatraṃ sarvakarmasu pūjitaṃ
pcdadhītya brāhmaṇaḥ snāyād rājānam abhiṣiñcayet
pabsarveṣāṃ ca dvijātīnāṃ sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
pcdśreṣṭhinaṃ sthāpayed deśe gaṇādhyakṣaṃ gaṇeśv api

dhaniṣṭhāyāṃ
pabnityaṃ śatabhiṣāyoge bhaiṣajyāni prayojayet
pcdkīrtikarma ca kurvīta sidhyanty ātharvaṇāni ca
pabprasārayec ca paṇyāni śauṇḍikaṃ ca prayojayet
pcdadadhiṃ khānāyet tatra tilamāṣāṃś ca vāpayet
pabsāmudrikāṇi paṇyāṇi nāvinaś ca prayojayet
pcdādeyaṃ ca tadā adadyād vyayaṃ caatra na kārayet
pabsandhipālān dvārapālāṃl lekhakāṃś ca prayojayet
pcdbhiṣakkarma ca kurvīta bhaiṣajyāni ca saṃharet

dvādaśāṅgulāyāṃ chāyāyām ādityaḥ parivartate
puṣyo rātriṃ nayati
jyeṣṭhāyām ādityo gato bhavati
hemantānāṃ caturthe
māse śravaṇām āvāsyaṃ bhavati
phalgunī pūrṇamāsyāṃ
trayodaśa muhūrto divaso bhavati
saptadaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ
daśāṅgulāyāṃ chāyāyām ādityaḥ parivartate
maghā rātriṃ nayati
āṣāḍhāyām ādityo gato bhavati
pgrīṣmāṇāṃ prathame māse uttarabhādrapadām āvāsyayaṃ bhavati
citrā pūrṇamāsyāṃ caturdaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati
ṣoḍaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ
 aṣṭāṅgulāyāṃ chāyāyām ādityaḥ parivartate
phalgunī rātriṃ nayati
śravaṇāyām ādityo gato bhavati
grīṣmāṇāṃ dvitīye māse aśvinī amāvāsyāyāṃ bhavati
viśākhā pūrṇamāsyāṃ
pañcadaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati
pañcadaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ
ṣaḍaṅgulāyāṃ chāyāyām ādityaḥ parivartate
citrā rātriṃ nayati
uttarāyāṃ bhādrapadāyām ādityo gato bhavati
grīṣmānāṃ tṛtīye māse kṛttikām amāvāsyāyāṃ bhavati
jyeṣṭhā pūrṇamāsyāṃ
ṣoḍaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati
caturdaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ
caturaṅgulāyāṃ chāyāyām ādityāḥ parivartate
viśākhā rātriṃ nayati
kṛttikāyām ādityo gato
bhavati grīṣmāṇāṃ caturthe māse mṛgaśirā amāvāsyāyāṃ bhavati
uttarāṣāḍhā pūrṇamāsyāṃ
saptadaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati
trayodaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ
madhyāhne dviaṅgulāyāṃ chāyāyām ādityaḥ parivartate
jyeṣṭhā rātriṃ nayati
puṣya ādityo gato bhavati
psaṃvatsaram anveṣaṇato muhūrtaviśeṣaṇaiḥ sarvāṇi caetāni nakṣatāṇi
bhāgānubhagenaamāvāsyayaṃ pūrṇamāsyaṃ ca yujyante
ūnarātrasya pūrṇarātrasya ca grahītavyaṃ
tatra tṛtīye varṣe adhiko māso yujyate
ṣaṇṇāṃ māsānām ahorātrāṇi samāni bhavanti
ataḥ ṣaṇmāsād divaso vadhate
ṣaṇmāsād rātrir  vardhate
ṣaṇmāsād divaso māse māse samam eva
hīyate ṣaṇmāsād rātrir māse māse parihīyate
pṣaṇmāsād ādityaḥ parivartate
uttarāṃ diśaṃ saṃcarati
ṣaṇmāsād dakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ
ṣaṇmāsāt samudr
e udakaparimāṇasya hrāso vṛddhiś ca bhavati
sūryagatyā candragatyā ca samudraudakavelāabhivṛddhir bhavati
atra gaṇanāpratijāgaraṇāsmaram ity evam eṣa saṃvatsaro vyākhyāto bhavati
grahaḥ
pcandra ādityaḥ śukro bṛhaspatiḥ śanaiścaro aṅgārako budhaś ca
ime grahāḥ
eṣāṃ grahāṇāṃ bṛhaspatiḥ saṃvatsarasthāyo
evaṃ śanaiścaro budho aṅgārakaḥ śukraś caime maṇḍalacāriṇaḥ
nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ
pbharaṇī kṛttikā rohiṇī mṛgaśirā etat sādhāraṇaṃ prathamaṃ maṇḍalaṃ
ārdrā punarvasuḥ puṣyo aśleṣā etat sādhāranaṃ dvitīyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ
maghā atha phalgunadvayaṃ hasto citrā etat sādhāraṇaṃ tṛtīyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ
svātī viśākhā anurādhā etat sādhāraṇaṃ caturthaṃ maṇḍalaṃ
jyeṣṭhā mūlāṣāḍhādvayam 
atra sarvāṇi mahābhāyāni bhavanti
idaṃ pañcamaṃ maṇḍalaṃ
abhijic chravaṇā dhaniṣṭhā śatabiṣā ubhe bhādrapade caitat sādhāraṇaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ maṇḍalaṃ
revatī avinī caitat sādhāraṇaṃ saptamaṃ maṇḍalaṃ
saṃvatsaram eteṣu yad yan nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ pīḍayati tasya tasya janapadasya sattvasya vā pīḍā nirdeṣṭavyā
pdvādaśamuhūrtāni divase dhruvāṇi dvādaśa rātrau
ṣaṇmuhūrtāḥ sañcāriṇaḥ
katame ṣaṭ
nairṛto varuṇo vāyavo bhargo devo raudro vicārī ca
itīme sañcāriṇaḥ ṣaṭ 
pathātra śrāvaṇe māse pūrṇe aṣṭādaśamuhūrte divase sūryaudaye ca caturojā nāma muhūrto bhavati
rohitasya ca muhūrtasya balasya caantare madhyāhno bhavati
sūryāvatāre tu vicārī nāma muhūrto bhavati
dvādaśamuhūrtāyāṃ rātrāv avatīrṇe sūrye ṣaṣṭhe muhūrte nayamano nāma muhūrto bhavati
ātāpāgnir evaṃ nāma muhūrto rātryavasāne bhavati
bhādrapade
māse pūrṇe saptadaśamuhūrte divase sūryaudaye ca caturojā evaṃ nāma muhūrtā bhavati
madhyāhne abhijito nāma muhūrto bhavati
 sūryāvatāre raudro nāma muhūrto bhavati
trayodaśamuhūrtāyāṃ rātrāv avatīrṇe sūrye vicārī nāma muhūrto bhavati
ardharātre mahābhayo vāyāvo nāma muhūrto bhavati
prātryavasāne ātapāgnir evaṃ nāma muhūrto bhavati
aśvayuje māse pūrṇe ṣoḍaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati
sūryaudaye caturojā nāma muhūrto bhavati
samudgatasya ca muhūrtasya abhijitasya caantare madhyāhno bhavati
sūryāvatāre bhargo devo nāma muhūrto bhavati
pcaturdaśamuhūrtāyāṃ rātrāv avatīrṇe sūrye raudro nāma muhūrto bhavati
abhijitasya ca muhūrtasya bhīṣamāṇasya ca muhūrtasya antareṇaardharātraṃ bhavati
rātryavasāne ātapāgnir evaṃ nāma muhūrto bhavati
pkārttike māse pūrṇe divasaḥ samarātrir bhavati
pañcadaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati pañcadaśamuhūrto rātriḥ
samāne ahorātre sūryaudaye caturojā evaṃ nāma muhūrto bhavati
saṃmukho nāma muhūrto bhavati madhyāhne
santato nāma muhūrtaḥ 
sūryāvatāre
rātrāv avatīrṇamātra sūrye bhrgo devo nāma muhūrto bhavati
ardharātre abhijin muhūrto bhavati
rātryavasāne ātapāgnir evaṃ nāma muhūrto bhavati
pmārgaśīrṣe māse ca pūrṇe caturdaśamuhūrte divase sūryaudaye caturojā evaṃ nāma muhūrto bhavati
viratasya saṃmukhasya ca muhūrtasyaantare madhyāhno bhavati
sūryaavatāre varuṇo nāma muhūrto bhavati
ṣoḍaśamuhūrtāyāṃ rātrāv avatīrṇamātre sūrye saṃtāpanaḥ saṃyamo nāma muhūrto bhavati
rākṣasasyābhijitasya ca muhūrtasyaantare ardharātraṃ
bhavati rātryavasāne ātapāgnir evaṃ nāma muhūrto bhavati
ppauṣamāse pūrṇe trayodaśamuhūrte divase sūryaudaye caturojā evaṃ nama muhūrto bhavati
madhyāhne virato nāma muhūrto bhavati
sūryāvatāre nairṛto nāma muhūrto bhavati
saptadaśamuhūrtāyāṃ rātrāv avatīrṇamātre sūrye varuṇo nāma muhūrto bhavati
ardharātre rākṣaso nāma muhūrto bhavti
rātryavasāne ātapāgnir evaṃ nāma muhūrto bhavati
pmāghamāse pūrṇe dvādaśamuhūrte divase sūryaudaye caturojā nāma muhūrto bhavati
sāvitrasya ca viratasya ca muhūrtasyaantareṇa madhyāhno bhavati
sūryāvatāre vijayo nāma muhūrto bhavati
aṣṭādaśamuhūrtāyāṃ rātrāv avatīrṇamātre sūrye nairṛto nāma muhūrto bhavati
gardabhasya muhūrtasya ca rākṣasasya caantaram ardharātraṃ bhavati
rātryavasāna
ātapāgnir evaṃ nāma muhūrto bhavati
pyathā śrāvaṇe tathā māghe
yathā bhādrapade tathā phālgune
yathā asvayuje tathā caitra
yathā kārttike tathā vaiśākhe
yathā mārgaśīrṣe tathā jyaiṣṭhe
yathā pauṣe tathā aṣāḍhe
evam eteṣāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ muhūrtānāṃ caritaṃ vicaritaṃ ca jñātavyaṃ
nakṣatravicaraṇaṃ nāma prathamo adhyāyāḥ

pcddṛśyante abhrā hi sandhyāyāṃ grastvā candradivākarau
pabtadā nabhasi jāyante meghā ḍāḍimbasannibhāḥ
pcdlakṣaṇaṃ tādṛśaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidyāt tānn indrakampitān
pefsa nirdeśo bhavet tatra maharṣer vacanaṃ yathā
pabatīva tatra viśvastaḥ sarvabījāni vāpayet
pcdvyavahārāṃś ca kurvīran nirbhayās tatra vāṇijāḥ
pefsarveṣāṃ bhūmikampānāṃ praśastā
indrakaṃpitāḥ
pabvepitāyāṃ tu medinyāṃ bhaved rūpam anantaraṃ
pcdsaptāhābhyantare tatra meghaḥ saṃcchādayen nabhaḥ
pabtato anubaddhā jāyante
abhrāḥ kauśeyasannibhāḥ
pcdanulomaṃ ca saṃyānti carantaḥ paścimāṃ diśaṃ
pabśiśumāraudrakāṇāṃ matsyamakarasannibhāḥ
pcddṛśyante abhrāś ca sandhyāyāṃ grastvā candradivākarau
pablakṣaṇaṃ tādṛśaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidyāt tāñ jalakampitān
pcdsa nirdeśo bhavet tatra maharṣer vacanaṃ yathā
pabsthāleṣu girikūṭeṣu kṣetreṣūpavaneṣu ca
pcdsthāpyante tatra bījāni nimne naśyanti vai tadā
pabpañkeṇaapi jalenaapi naśyeyū rajasāapi vā
pcdeteṣāṃ bhūmikampānāṃ praśastā jalakampitāḥ
pabvepitāyāṃ tu medinyāṃ bhaved rūpam anantaraṃ
pcdsaptāhābhyantare tatra vātā vānti sudāruṇāḥ
pabdṛśyate kapilā sandhyā candrasūryau tu lohitāu
pcdlakṣaṇaṃ tādṛśaṃ dṛṣṭvā jānīyād vāyukampitān
pabtato bhavati nirdeśo maharṣer vacanaṃ yathā
pcdna tatra pravaset prājña
ātmānaṃ caatra gopayet
pabguhyam āvaraṇaṃ kuryāt prākāraparikhāṃ khanet
pcdprātisīmā virudhyante narāṇāṃ jāyate bhayaṃ
pabeteṣāṃ bhūmikampanaṃ sarveṣāṃ kīrtitā guṇāḥ
pcdviśeṣeṇa manuṣyāṇāṃ nirmitā vāyukampitāḥ
pabkampitāyāṃ tu medinyāṃ bhaved rūpam anantaraṃ
pcdsaptāhābhyantarāt tatra
ulkāpātāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
pabsandhyā ca lohitā bhāti candrasūryau tu lohitau
pcdlakṣaṇaṃ tādṛśaṃ dṛṣṭvā vijñeyā
agnikampitāḥ
pabagnir dahati kāṣṭhāni rakṣitāni dhanāni ca
pcddṛśyante dhūmaśikharāḥ śastraṃ ca svidyate bhṛśaṃ
pabvīṇāś ca divi dṛśyante navamāsān na varṣati
pcdeteṣāṃ bhūmikampānāṃ jaghanyā
agnikampitāḥ
pajayati ahani pūrve kṣatriyān pārthivāṃś ca
pbhayagajarathamukhyān mantriṇo madhyamaahne
āparaahṇe gopaśūn vaiśyaśūdrān
pcdpradahati niśisandhyā taskaraanantavāsān
parajanim iha pradoṣe hiṃsate mlecchasaṃghān
pbstriyam api ca napuṃsaś caardharātreṣv anantān
pckṛṣivaṇig upajīvyān hanti yāme tṛtīye
pdvyathayati surapakṣaṃ raudrakarmaantakṛṣṇe
papradahati śaśipakṣe yājñikaṃ brahmakṣatraṃ
pbśrapayati śucivṛttām eva dharme pradhānān
pcviduṣi ca mṛdubhāvaṃ vindate yo hy adhīte
pdsa bhavati nṛpapūjyo bāhmaṇo devadarśī
pabbṛhaspateś ca catvāri samāni śubhakarmaṇā
pcdcatvāri sūryakarmāṇi tulyāni śukrakarmaṇā
pefsomakarmāṇi catvāri brahmakarma ca tatsamaṃ
payaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārin bhūmikampanirdeśo nāmaadhyāyaḥ
 vyādhisamutthānaṃ
patha bhoḥ puṣkarasārin amīṣām aṣṭāviṃśatīnāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ rogautpattiṃ nāmaadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāmi

 bandhananirmokṣaḥ

kathayatu bhagavān
pkṛttikāsu bhoḥ puṣkarasārin baddho vā ruddho vā trirātreṇa mokṣyatiiti vaktavyaḥ
rohiṇyāṃ baddho vā ruddho vā trirātreṇa mokṣyatiiti
mṛgaśirasi baddho vā ruddho vā ekaviṃśati rātreṇa mokṣyatiiti
ārdrāyāṃ baddho vā ruddho vā ardhamāsena mokṣyatiiti
punarvasau ruddho vā baddho vā saptarātrena
puṣye trirātreṇa
aśleṣāyāṃ triṃśadrātreṇa
maghāsu ṣoḍaśarātreṇa
citrāyāṃ saptarātreṇa
svātyāṃ daśarātreṇa
viśākhāyāṃ ṣaḍviṃśadrātreṇa
anurādhāyām ekatriṃśad rātreṇa
jyeṣṭhāyām aṣṭādaśarātreṇa
mūle ṣaṭtriṃśad rātreṇa
pūrvāṣāḍhāyāṃ caturdaśarātreṇa
uttarāṣāḍhāyāṃ caturdaśarātreṇa
abhijiti ṣaḍrātreṇa

 tilakaadhyāyaḥ
patha boḥ puskarasārin tilakaadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmi
tac chrūyatāṃ
kathayatu bhagavān
pmūrdhni tu yasyās tilako asti sūkṣmaḥ snigdho bhavet padmasamānavarṇaḥ
prājā tu tasyā bhavatiiha bhartā stanaupariṣṭāt pratibimbam āhuḥ
pabśīrṣe tu yasyās tilakaalakaḥ syāt sūkṣmo bhaved añjanacūrṇavarṇaḥ
pcdsenāpatis tasyā bhaved dhi bhartā stanaantare asyāḥ pratibimbakaṃ syāt
pabbhrūvontare asyās tilakaalakaḥ syād duṣcāriṇīṃ tāṃ pramadāṃ vadanti
pcdpañcaeva tasyāḥ patayo bhavanti bahvannapānaṃ labhate ca nārī
pabgaṇḍasya nāsādikam adhyadeśe bhavec ca bimbaṃ tilakasya yasyāḥ
pcdtāṃ śokabhājaṃ pramadāṃ vadanti romapradeśe pratibimbam āhuḥ
pabkarṇe tu yasyās tilakaalakaḥ syād bahuśrutāṃ tāṃ pramadāṃ vadanti
pcdbahuśrūtāṃ tāṃ śrutidhāriṇīṃ ca trike tu yasyāḥ pratibimbakaṃ syāt
pabyasyauttaroṣṭhe tilakaalakaḥ syāt tāṃ bhinnasatyāṃ pramadāṃ vadanti
pcdkṛcchreṇa sā vai labhate hi vṛttim ūrau tu tasyās tilabimbam āhuḥ
pabyasyā adharoṣṭhe tilakaalakaḥ syād duścāriṇīṃ tāṃ pramadāṃ vadanti
pcdmiṣṭaannapānaṃ bahu ṛcchate sā tathā hi guhye pratibimbakaṃ syāt
pabcibuke tu yasyās tilakaalakaḥ syād duścāriṇīṃ tāṃ pramadāṃ vadanti
pcdmiṣṭaannapānaṃ bahu sā labheta guhye dvitīyaṃ pratibimbakaṃ syāt
payaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasāriṃs tilakaadhyāyo nāmaadhyāyaḥ

kathayatu bhavān triśaṅkko
pakṛttikāsu naro jātas tejasvī priyasāhasaḥ
pbbhavec chūras tathā caṇḍaḥ priyavādī ca mānavaḥ
parohiṇyāṃ puruṣo jāto dhanavān dharmikas tathā
pbvyavasāyī sthiraḥ śūro dhruvaṃ caasya sadā mukhaṃ
pabjāto mṛgaśire yas tu mṛduḥ saumyas tu mānavaḥ
pcddarśanīyo bhavec caasau strīkāntas tu viśeṣataḥ
pabārdrājātas tu hiṃsātmā caṇḍaḥ paramajalpakaḥ
pcdrodrakarmā bhavec caasāv īścaraś ca śatair mahān
pabjātaḥ punarvasau yas tu hy alolo buddhimān naraḥ
pcddharmaśīlo bhavec caasau jātakrodhaś ca mānavaḥ
pabpuṣyeṇa puruṣo jātas tejasvī brāhmaṇo bhavet
pcdkṣatriyaś ca bhaved rājā vaiśyasūdrau ca pūjitau
pabśvasanaḥ krodhanaḥ krūro hy aśleṣāsambhavo naraḥ
pcddurmanuṣyaś ca caṇḍaś ca
iti sarvam ihādiśet
pabbahuprajñaḥ śrāddhakaro bahubhāgyas tathāeva ca
pcddhanavān dhānyavān bhogī maghāsu puruṣo bhavet
pabpūrvaphālgunījātas tu yaḥ kaścit puruṣo bhavet
pcdardham abucchiśīlaś ca gurudārāabhimardakaḥ
pabuttarāyāṃ tu phālgunyāṃ jāto bhavati bhogavān
pcddivyajñānaś ca vijñāne puruṣaḥ subhago bhavet
pabhaste jātaś ca śuddhaātmā vikrānto mṛdubhojanaḥ
pcdsenāpatyam ca kurute asteyakarmā bhaved asau
pabcitrāsu jātaś citrāakṣas tathā citrakathākaraḥ
pcddarśanīyo bahustrīkaś citraśīlo bhaven naraḥ
pabsvātyāṃ ca puruṣo jāto bandhuś lāghī cicakṣaṇaḥ
pcdmṛdukaḥ pānaśauṇḍaś ca mitrakārī vicāravān
pabviśākhāsu naro jātas tejasvī dravyavān mahān
pcdśūro vikramavān dakṣaḥ subhagaś ca bhaved asau
pabanurādhāudbhavo martyo mitravān saṃgrahī naraḥ
pcdśuciś caeva kṛtajñaś ca dharmaātmā ca bhavec ca saḥ
pabjyeṣṭhāsu puruṣo jāto mitravān abhijāyate
pcddhanurvedaabhirāmaś ca nārīṣu kurute manaḥ
pabmūleṣu puruṣo jāto akṛtajñaḥ syād adharmikaḥ
pcddṛḍho vīro bhavec caasau kilviṣī ca sa mānavaḥ
pabāṣāḍhāsu ca pūrvāsu matsarī calitaindriyaḥ
pcdmatsyamāṃsapriyaś caapi ghātakaḥ syāt sa mānavaḥ
pabsaanukrośaś ca dātā ca vidyāniṣṭhaḥ suhṛjjanaḥ
pcdviśvadaive naro jāto bhaved api ca niścitaḥ
pabācāryaḥ śāstrakartā ca viśvāsī ca kriyāparaḥ
pcdśravaṇe jata
āyuṣmān śrīmāṃś ca puruṣo bhavet
pabanavasthitacittaś ca ccitradravyaś ca mānavaḥ
pcddhaniṣṭhāsu bhavej jātaḥ puruṣaḥ sarvaśāṅkitaḥ
pabvāruṇe yadi nakṣatre jāto bhavati mānavaḥ
pcdparuṣo kveṣaśīlaś ca parivādī ca sarvaśaḥ
pabjāto bhādrapadāyāṃ tu pūrvasyām iha mānavaḥ
pcdcāritraguṇayuktaś ca kṛtajño mukharas tathā
pabuttarasyāṃ naro jāto bhaviṣyati vicakṣaṇaḥ
pcdmedhāvī bahv apatyaś ca dharmaśīlo mahādhanaḥ
pabrevatyāṃ puruṣo jāto dharmaātmā jñātisevakaḥ
pcddaridro alpadhano nityaṃ dāyako naanusūyakaḥ
pabaśvinyāṃ puruṣo jāto bhavay ativicakṣaṇaḥ
pcdmahājanapriyaś caapi śūraś ca subhagaś ca saḥ
pabbharaṇyāṃ puruṣo jātaḥ pāpācāro avicakṣaṇaḥ
pcdkandarpe dātukāmaś ca parataś caupajīvakaḥ
payaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārinn nakṣatrajanmaguṇo nāmaadhyāyaḥ

uefvidyuto vāatha dṛśyante tadā vidyāj janakṣayaṃ
uabaśvinyām arkato dhūmo nirgacchann api chādayet
ucdanāvṛṣṭiṃ tadā vidyāt pūrṇavarṣāṇi dvādaśa
uabbharaṇyāṃ māghamāse tu pītasūryo atha dṛśyate
ucdsamantād vadhyate rāṣṭraṃ madhye durbhikṣam ādiśet
uabphālgune kṛttikāyāṃ tu
āditye parikho yadi
ucdnaśyanti karvaṭās tatra yadi devo na varṣati
uabcaitramāse yadā puṣye sūrye kṛṣṇāṃ pradṛśyate
ucdacirodayakāle tu kṣitipālo avarudhyate
uabvaiśākhamāse caardrāyām ādityaḥ pratisūryakaḥ
ucdsaṃgrāmaṃ tatra jānīyād ubhau ghātyete pārthivau
uabgṛhyetāṃ candrasūryau vā jyaiṣṭhe bharaṇijyeṣṭhayoḥ
ucdsaamātyo vadhyate rājā rāṣṭre durbhikṣam ādiśet
uabāṣāḍhe ca yadāāditye pūrvabhādrapade sthite
ucdsāyāhne dṛśyate atyarthaṃ lohito maṇḍale braṇaḥ
uabparacakreṇa tadrāṣṭraṃ ṣaṇmāsān pīḍyate tadā
ucdkṣitipālaś ca saamātyaḥ putradāreṇa vadhyate
uabpūrvāyāṃ cauttarāṣāḍhāyām āṣāḍhe gṛhyate śaśī
ucdvidyād durbhikṣakalaha rogāṃś caatra vinirdiśet
uabmāse atha śrāvaṇe mūle candrasūryau na bhāsataḥ
ucdsphuliṅgāś caatra dṛśyante vidyād rogabhayaṃ mahat
uabmāse aśvayuji gṛhyetāṃ ekapakṣendubhāskarop
ucdrājaputrasahasrāṇāṃ tadā jāyeta saṃkṣayaḥ
uabalakṣaṇo niḥprakāśaḥ pūrṇamāsyāṃ tu kārttike
ucdcandrasūryāv agnivarṇau raktavarṇe nabhastale
uabravivad bhāti tadrāṣṭraṃ vinaśyeta punaḥ punaḥ
ucdrājñāṃ vidyād dhatānāṃ vai bhūmiḥ pāstyati śoṇitaṃ
uabbharaṇyāṃ māghamāse tu kṛṣṇo vāyuḥ samutthitaḥ
ucdchādayec candrasūryau tu śīghraṃ rāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati
uabmāse tu phālgune vāyuḥ pāṃśuvarṣaṃ savidyutaṃ
ucdvadhyante pūrvarājānaḥ pratiṣṭhante tathāapare
uabsahaādityena candre atha yadā kaścid grahaś caret
ucdvāyur vā viṣamo vātii vidyād rājavadhaṃ tadā
uabaśanyulke tu vaiśākhe
ādityena sahautthite
ucdṣaṇmāsaabhyantareṇaatha rāṣṭre vyasanam ādiśet
uabjyeṣṭhamāse yadāādityo grahato nirgato bhavet
ucdādityasyaupaghātena grahāḥ sarve atha pīḍitāḥ
uabjyeṣṭhe ca pāṃśur varṣeta
ādityaḥ pariviṣyate
ucdkṣitipālasahasrāṇāṃ eka
ekas tu vadhyate
uabāṣāḍhe vāyavo vānti gacchanto bharaṇīsthitāḥ
ucdudapānāni śuṣyante sarvaśasyaṃ ca śuṣyati
uabśrāvaṇe vāyavaḥ pītāḥ sadā kṛṣṇaṃ nabhastalaṃ
ucdbhayaṃ tatra vijānīyāt samantāt samupasthitaṃ
uabśrāvaṇe varṣate hy agniḥ pūrvabhādrapade divā
ucdmeghāḥ śabdam utkurvanti rogadurbhikṣam ādiśet
uabyadā bhādrapade māse nabhaḥ syāc channagarjitaṃp
ucdparacakraṃ tadā rāṣṭre harate dhanasañcayaṃ
uabaśvayuji vātavṛṣṭiḥ syād āgatyauttarāṃ diśaṃ
ucdpātayec caevam āghātaṃ kṛtsnaṃ rāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati
uabkārttike śuklatrayodaśyāṃ yadā candre dhanur bhavet
ucdsamantān naśyate rāṣṭraṃ madhye durbhikṣam ādiśet
uabulkāpātā hy aśanayo māghamāse bhavanti vā
ucdaśvinyāṃ viṣaye tatra prajā aśvāsena vadhyate
uabmāse tu phālgune yatra
āgnivarṣaṃ nabhastalāt
ucdbhavec chabdas tadākāśe tadrāṣṭraṃ naśyate laghu
uabsvātyāṃ caitre yadā varṣaṃ niruddhaṃ vātavarṣitaṃ
ucddṛśyataindradhanuḥ kṣipraṃ nagaraṃ tad vinaśyate
uabbharaṇyāṃ jyeṣṭhamāse tu śabda
uttarato bhavet
ucdpītavarṇaṃ tadākāśaṃ paracakrabhayaṃ bhavet
uabāṣāḍhe māsi puṣye atha dṛśyante vyogni vidyutaḥ
ucdsatṛṇaudakavṛṣṭibhis tribhāgaṃ mucyate prajā
uabśrāvaṇe tu yadā mūle bahu devaḥ pravarṣati
ucddṛśyataindradhanus tatra kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahadbhayaṃ
uabmāse bhādrapade yatra nirghātaḥ patati kṣitau
ucdsukṛcchrā vāyavo vānti mahadrogabhayaṃ tadā
uabmāse bhādrapade puṣye vidigbhyo niścared dhvaniḥ
ucdkṣatriyaḥ kupyate kṣipraṃ vipakṣā tu datā prajā
uabbharaṇyām aśvayuje śabda upariṣṭād bhaved yadi
ucdsatṛṇaṃ cautsṛjet pāṃśuṃ tāpasānāṃ mahadbhayaṃ
uabkārttike tu yadāārdrāyāṃ śabdaḥ śrayeta bhairavaḥ
ucdcatuṣpadaḥ kārṣakāṇāṃ mṛtyuṃ tatra vinirdiśet
uabmārgaśīrṣe dhaniṣṭhāyāṃ tūryaśabdo ambare bhavetp
ucdvātāturas tadā rāṣṭre vyādhir bhavati dāruṇaḥ
uabpauṣamāse yadā svātyāṃ śabdo bhavati bhairavaḥ
ucdabhīkṣṇaṃ vidyud ākāśe paṇḍitānāṃ mahadbhayaṃ
uabmāghe śukle tu nirghāto nityaṃ śāmyed vasundharāṃ
ucdjānīyāt tṛtīye varṣe sakalaṃ rāṣṭravibhramaṃ
uabjyeṣṭhāyāṃ phālgune māse kṛṣṇavāyuḥ samākulaḥ
ucdabhīkṣṇaṃ kampate bhūmir brahmacāribhayaṃ tadā
uabpūrvabhādrapadāyāṃ tu caitre kampet kṣitir divā
ucdtasmin varṣe ca tadrāṣṭre parasainyān mahadbhayaṃ
uabpūrvāyāṃ ced āṣāḍhāyāṃ rātrau caitre ca niścalet
ucdasibhir hanyate rājā hanyate ca mahājanaḥ
uabvaiśākhe kampitā bhūmiḥ kṛṣṇapakṣe hy abhīkṣṇaśaḥ
ucdanāvṛṣṭyā tu durbhikṣaṃ māsān ṣaṭ tatra nirdiśet
uabjyeṣṭhe māse bharaṇyāṃ tu divā kamped vasundharā
ucdvidyād yodhasahasrāṇāṃ mahī pāsyati śoṇitaṃ
uabjyeṣṭhe māse yadā mūle rātrau bhūmiḥ prakampate
ucdpratyanto vadhyate rājā rāṣṭre baliṃ samādiśet
uabāṣāḍhe kampate bhūmiḥ puṣyanakṣatrasaṃsthite
ucdśasyaṃ vinaśyate tatra kalikarma ca jāyate
uabprakampante yadā caityā
ādrāyāṃ vā maghāsu vā
ucdjvaleyuḥ prapateyur vā naśyed rāṣṭraṃ tadā laghu
uabcaityā yatra prakampante hasanti ca namanti ca
ucdsarāṣṭraḥ kṣitipas tatra na cirān nāśam arcchati
uabśrāvaṇe kampate bhūmiḥ pūrvabhādrapadāsthitep
ucdsadā parājito rājā caurarāṣṭre ca vadhyate
uabkārttike kṣitikampena yadā caityaṃ viśīryate
ucddvāraṃ vā nagarasyaatha bhūyiṣṭhaṃ naśyate prajā
uabvāme vā kaṣīṇe candroḥ śṛṅge tiṣṭhed bṛhaspatiḥ
ucdmahābhogā vinaśyeyuḥ prakāśāḥ pṛthivīśvarāḥ
uabsūryācandramasoḥ sṛṅge lohitaaṅgo yadā aruhet
ucdkrūraakṣamantrikāt pīḍāṃ pratyantānāṃ vinirdiśet
uabśanaiścaro yadā śṛṅge somasyaabhiruhet tadā
ucdjñeyaṃ rogabhayaṃ ghoraṃ durbhikṣaṃ caatra nirdiśet
uabrāhuṇā nigṛhītas tu caullkayā hanyate śaśī
ucdṣaṇmāsaabhyantarāt tatra rājño vyasanam ādiśet
uabyasya caivaatha nakṣatre śaśī sūryo vigṛhyate
ucdrāhuṇā kṣitiyo rājyaiḥ saha pīḍām avāpnuyāt
uabrājño vai caatha nakṣatre candraṃ ketur yadā viśet
ucdpratyantarājabhiḥ sārdhaṃ śastrām ūrcchāṃ vinirdiśet
uabcandramadhyagataḥ śukraḥ phālgunyātha maghā yadā
ucdsarvadhānyāni śuṣyeyus tadā rogaṃ vinirdiśet
uabbṛhaspatiś ca śukraś ca lohitaaṅgaḥ śanaiścaraḥ
ucdlikhyanti somaśṛṅgasya tadā vidyān mahadbhayaṃ
uabdhūmaketur mahābhāgaḥ puṣyam āruhya tiṣṭhati
ucdcaturdiśaṃ tadā viṃcyāt paracakraiḥ parābhavaṃ
uabmaghāyāṃ lohitaaṅgo vā śravaṇe vā bṛhaspatiḥ
ucdtiṣṭhet saṃvatsaratrīṇi bhayaṃ vidyāt samāgaraṃ
uabtiṣṭhec chukro atha rohiṇyāṃ jyeṣṭhe māse kathaṃcana
ucdvyākuryān niyatam atra kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahadbhayaṃ
uabviśākhāyāṃ samīpasthau bṛhaspatiśanaiścaraup
ucdsomo vā raviṇā sārdhaṃ paracakrabhayaṃ tadā
uabkākāḥ śyenāś ca bṛdhrāś ca vaseyuḥ sahitā mudā
ucdmaithunaṃ vāritaṃ veyuḥ paraiḥ saha raṇas tadā
uabśyeno hastinivāse vā
abhirohet punaḥ punaḥ
ucdparacakreṇa yuddhaṃ tu bhavec caapi punaḥ punaḥ
uabkanyā prasūyate yatra caturhastā catustanī
ucdstrīṇām eva bhavet tatra maraṇaṃ hy atidāruṇaṃ
uabgarbhasthā dārakā yatra hasanti ca vadanti ca
ucdtasya deśasya jānīyād vināśaṃ samupasthitaṃ
uabekapādāṃ stripādāṃś ca caturaṅgāṃs tathāeva ca
ucdnāryo yatra prasūyante rājño vyasanam ādiśet
uabsūyante vikṛtān garbhān santānān bhayavyañjanān
ucdpramadā yatra deśe tu rājā tatra vinaśyati
uablaghuhastaśīrṣamukhān mānuṣaṃ kāyam aśritān
ucdpramadā yatra sūyante rāṣṭraṃ tatra vinaśyati
uabkharāś ca mahiṣāś caapi paśavo atha tathāvidhāḥ
ucddvitriśīrṣāḥ prasūyante deśe yatra sa naśyati
uabśṛgālaśvānamakarahayarūpāś ca mānavāḥ
ucdjāyante yatra deśe tu sa deśo laghu naśyati
uabpādāv ubhau yadā vaiśyā gurviṇī saṃprasūyate
ucddeśasya vilayaṃ brūyāt paracakreṇa dāruṇaṃ
uabpūrvārdhaḥ pakṣinarayor garbho yatra prasūyate
ucdrājā vā rājāmātyo vā saha deśena naśyati
uabkumbhāṇḍo jāyate yatra dvisukho atha caturmukhaḥp
ucdtrinetras trimukho vāapi vidyāt tatra mahadbhayaṃ
uabsaukareṇa tu vakreṇa śarīraṃ mānuṣaṃ yadi
ucdsūtaṃ caturdiśaṃ rāṣṭraṃ hanyāt tatra na saṃśayaḥ
uabādityasya tu rūpeṇa mānuṣo yatra jāyate
ucdvibhramāt sakalaṃ rāṣṭraṃ vināśam upagacchati
uabuttānaśāyī bālas tu deśaṃ yatra dvijottamaḥ
ucddṛṣṭaḥ pravyāharan vedān kṣipraṃ deśo vinaśyatei
uabkukṣiṃ bhitvā yadā bālo garbhān niṣkramate svayaṃ
ucdatrāṇāṃ mātaraṃ kṛtvā sa deśo naśyate laghu
uabgarbhasthāḥ sūkarā
uṣṭrāḥ sarpāś ca śakunis tathā
ucdstrīṇāṃ garbhāt prasūyante deśe tu bhayam ādiśet
uabpauruṣaṃ gārdabhaṃ caatha saukaraṃ caardhavigrahaṃ
ucdgāvo yatra prasūyante nirdiśed bhayam āgataṃ
uabnārī gṛhṇāti garbhaṃ vā
adṛṣṭastanarūpiṇī
ucdvināśaṃ tasya deśasya sanṛpasya vinirdiśet
uabjaṭī dīrghanakho yatra sukṛṣṇaḥ paruṣacchaviḥ
ucdsajano jāyate yatra rāṣṭraṃ sādhipatiṃ dahet
uabagrīvā dantasahitā jāyante yatra bālakāḥ
ucdśuṣyeta sakalaṃ śasyaṃ janaś ca vilayaṃ vrajet
uabekabāhuraśīrṣo atha garbho yatra prasūyate
ucdsvayaṃ kṣubhyeta tadrāṣṭraṃ vinaśyeta na saṃśayaḥ
uabphale phalaṃ yadā paśyet puṣpe vā puṣpam āśritaṃ
ucdgarbhāḥ sraveyur nārīṇāṃ yuvarājaś ca vadhyate
uabakāle pādapā yatra puṣpyanti ca phalanti cap
ucdlatā gulmo atha vallī vā deśe tatra bhayaṃ bhavet
uabvṛkṣaupariṣṭāt paśyed vā sravantam ātmaśoṇitam
ucdkūjamānaṃ pataṅgaṃ vā tadā vidyān mahadbhayaṃ
uabvṛkṣāṇāṃ maṇḍapānāṃ vā chāyā na parivartate
ucdcaturvarṇabhayaṃ tatra kalikarma ca jāyate
uabpuṣpyegruḥ pādapā yatra vividhāḥ puṣpajātayaḥ
ucdkalpavṛkṣaprakṛtayas tato vidyān mahadbhayaṃ
uabanāvartaṃ yadā puṣpaṃ phalaṃ caapi pradṛśyate
ucdvināśaṃ tasya deśasya durbhikṣaṃ kalahaṃ vadet
uabsthānāsthānaṃ gatā vṛkṣā dṛśyeyur yatra kutracit
ucdpūrvapratiṣṭhitā rājā na cireṇa vicālyate
uabdaivaasuraṃ ca saṃgrāmaṃ paśyed adbhutadarśanaṃ
ucdśastraṃ mūrcchayate tatra taskaraiś caapi pūrvavat
uabkampate rudate śāstā gacchan vā yatra dṛśyate
ucdparacakrāt tadā vidyād atyarthaṃ tatprarājayaṃ
uabdevatā yatra deśe tu nṛtyanti ca hasanti ca
ucdaśrūṇi pātayeyur vā tadā vidyān mahadbhayaṃ
uabdevatā yatra krīḍanti jvalanti nimiṣanti vā
ucdcaleyur athavā yatra kṣitipo anyo bhavet tadā
uabśivaliṅaṃ yadā kamped gagane vāatha dṛśyate
ucdnimajjate dharaṇyāṃ vā dhruvaṃ rājavadho bhavet
uabpratimāḥ parivartante dhūmāyante rudanti ca
ucdprasvidyeyuḥ pradhāveyur anyo rājā bhaviṣyati
uabacalo vā calet sthānāc calaṃ vāapy acalaṃ bhavet
ucdamātyo hanti rājānaṃ kalahaṃ caatra nirdiśet
uabvamanti rudhiraṃ kanyā namante vā diśo daśap
ucdayuktā vā pravartante kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahadbhayaṃ
uabvarṣate kusumaṃ yatra raktavindum athaapi vā
ucdprāṇino vividhān vāapi vidyāc caurabhayaṃ tadā
uabyūpāḥ purāṇā nigamā devaāgārāṇi caitiyāḥ
ucdnagarāṇy atha dhūmyante kṣipraṃ rājā vinaśyati
uabindur vā dīpavṛkso vā dīpo yatra na dīpyate
ucdrājyakāmaḥ kumāro vā kṣubhyed viṭapako api vā
uabantaḥpure yadā nīḍāṃ kurvate madhumakṣikāḥ
ucdastraṃ vāapi gṛhaṃ dahyād rājño vyasanam ādiśet
uabpated antaḥpure vidyud vṛkṣe vāapy āśrame tathā
ucdpuri caityacchāyāyāṃ vā rājārthe patitā hi sā
uabprākāre vā ayudhāgāre gopurāsthānakeṣu vā
ucdvāyasaḥ kurute nīḍaṃ saamātyo dhvaṃsate nṛpaḥ
uabanāhatebhyas tūryehbhyaḥ svayaṃ śabdo viniścaret
ucdsvacakrakṣobhadoṣeṇa sarvaṃ rāṣṭraṃ vilupyate
uabmāṃsaśoṇitavarṣaṃ vā patrapuṣpaphalāni vā
ucdyadābhivarṣet tadvarṣaṃ cakrai rāṣṭraṃ vilupyate
uabmadhuphāṇitapuṣpāṇi gandhavarṣāṇy athaapi vā
ucddiśo dāhāś ca dṛśyeyur māradurbhikṣalakṣaṇaṃ
uabmeghaḥ samantato garjed upavarṣet sacātakaṃ
ucdśoṇitaṃ sakarakaṃ syāt tadā vidyāt parād bhayaṃ
uabvidyuc ca patate ghorā karakāṇāṃ ca varṣaṇaṃ
ucdgandharvanagaraṃ caatha dṛṣṭvā vidyān mahadbhayaṃ
uabśaśī śoṇitasaṃkāśo madhye kṛṣṇo vivarṇavānp
ucdsāmantakena pīḍyate vidyād rāṣṭre mahadbhayaṃ
uabpradīpitaagnisaṃkāśo yadā dṛśyeta candramāḥ
ucdgaganaṃ dahyate tatra lokapīḍā jvareṇa ca
uabyadā gairikasaṃkāśaḥ kṣipram evaupaśāmyati
ucdvarṣaṇasyaāgamo vidyād yadi vāyuḥ pravāyate
uabsandhyāyāṃ dhūmravarṇāyāṃ dṛśyetenduś ca bhāskaraḥ
ucdvicchinno brahmarūpeṇa varṣaṃ tatra vinirdiśed
uabnāpsu majjati naapy agnau pūrvavac ca na dṛśyate
ucdagnir utpatsyate tatra koṣṭhaāgāraṃ daheta saḥ
uabdhvajaagre vāyaso yatra lambapakṣo vidhāvate
ucdudakaṃ saṃharet kṣipram agnitaḥ sumahadbhayaṃ
uabjalaṃ jājvalyamānaṃ tu matsyo nirdahati svayaṃ
ucdanāvṛṣṭiṃ tadā brūyād durbhikṣaṃ ca mahadbhayaṃ
uabpuradvāre yadāāgacchet svayam āraṇyako mṛgaḥ
ucdcakradvaye api durbhikṣaṃ rāṣṭre rogaṃ ca nirdiśet
uabtriśīrṣaḥ pañcaśīrṣo vā yadā sarpo atha dṛśyate
ucdanāvṛṣṭyā tadā vidyāt sarvaśasyaṃ vinaśyati
uabkuśūlo yatra dṛśyeta kampayan tu vasundharāṃ
ucdkoṣṭhaāgārāṇi naśyeyur ye caanye dhanasañcayāḥ
uabsarpa udyataśīrṣas tu yudhyate puruṣaiḥ saha
ucdcakradvayād rogataś ca vidyāt tatra mahadbhayaṃ
uabbila ekatra bahavaḥ sarpāḥ supariveṣṭitāḥ
ucdśastramṛtyuṃ tadā vidyāt kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahadbhayaṃ
uabniścaranty avadhānena khaḍgāḥ prajvalitā yadā
ucdtatas taṃ na cirāt paśyet saṃgrāmaṃ pratyupasthitaṃ
uabkākaḥ śyenaś ca gṛdhro vā yasya nīyeta mūrdhani
ucdṣaṇmāsaabhyantare rājā mriyate sapurohitaḥ
uabprāsādāś ca prakampante śaraṇāni gṛhāṇi ca
ucdmahābalaṃ ca vadhyeta rāṣṭrasya rājapālakaḥ
uabvajrauddhṛtā diśaḥ sarvāḥ kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdiśaṃ
ucdvarṣeyuḥ śoṇitaṃ yatra kṣitipālo atra vadhyate
uabsūryasyaudayakāle tu maholkā nipated yadā
ucdrājaputrasahasrāṇāṃ bhūmiḥ pāsyāti śoṇitaṃ
uabvṛkṣāḥ sarpāḥ prakampeyur mucyeyus tvaco vā tathā
ucdsarvasmin eva rāṣṭre tu vidyāc chatrubhayaṃ mahat
uabdine hy ulkāprayuktir vā jvalantī yadi dṛśyate

uabasiṃ prajvalitaṃ paśyet tomaraṃ cakram eva ca

uaṣṭāviṃśatiḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatrāṇi prakīrtitāni

ucdśuṣkavṛkṣe niṣīditvā tatra vidyān mahābhayaṃ
uabbhītas trastaḥ parītaś ca yas tu vyāharate khagaḥ
ucdparibādhan diśaḥ sarvās tatra bhayam upasthitaṃ
uabgacchantaṃ samanugacchet puraḥ sthitvā tu vyāharet
ucdna tatra gamanaṃ kkuryān mārgam atra praśātanaṃ
uabvāstumadhye pratisthāne kṣāmaṃ dīnaṃ ca vyāharet
ucdvyādhiṃ tatra vijānīyād vāse vā gṛhasvāmināṃ
uabśakaṭasya yathā śabdaṃ viśrabdhaṃ vāśati vāyasaḥ
ucddūrād abhyāgataṃ jñātvā prasiddhiṃ caabhinirdiśet
uabgargare ghaṭake caeva sthālikapiṭhareṣu vā

uabāsane śayane vāapi sthito vāśati vāyasaḥ
ucdprasiddhaṃ gamanaṃ brūyāt proṣitena samāgamaḥ
uabbrahmasthāne niṣīditvā dhruvaṃ vāśati vāyasaḥ
ucdarthalābhaṃ vijānīyād dhanalābhaṃ ca ākaret

uabdevatādevatānāṃ ca devasyaupavanāni ca

uabpātraṃ ca pātrakaṃ caeva mṛttikāvarabhājanaṃp

ucdabhyantare saptarātrān maraṇaṃ tasya nirdiśet
